Picture 2: The baby found a cockroach and excitedly shared it with me. Watching cockroaches crawl under the sofa was so disgusting that I didn‚Äôt record the video.
Figure 3: Welcome to browse the records of the camera for evidence collection.
I have reported the above to the local health bureau, but I think it will have no effect.

Room: Because it was a last-minute trip, I just booked a twin bed. The room was very small, on a low floor, and the view was a chimney. But it is indeed designed very reasonably. It's just not suitable for young babies to live in. It's all made of steel and corners, so bumps are inevitable. The baby bumped his head once and his arm twice. You can't install the bumper *****s yourself, so it's dangerous. The fence is L-shaped. If you want to use it, you have to have a twin bed and a big bed, so there is no point in booking a twin bed.
Secondly, the water temperature in the bathroom is unstable and drops during peak water use periods, making bathing very uncomfortable. The door is not soundproof, and the shouting in the corridor can be heard very clearly. The windows are not soundproofed and there are occasional events downstairs which are very noisy.

Facilities: This is the most profit-oriented Shangri-La I have ever stayed at. The gym is open to the outside, the children's playground is open to the outside, and the outdoor children's amusement facilities are public... Although the guest room area can only be entered by swiping a card, there is basically nothing except the small room and the spacious guest room meeting area (you have to listen to other people's meetings when entering the room area...) What are the exclusive facilities for hotel guests. After the epidemic, consumption has been downgraded, and it is understandable that hotels need to make profits to survive. But how to downgrade decently may require some knowledge. The traditional hotel industry is undergoing transformation, but if the soul is lost, it will not look good.

Others: There is basically no service training. Everyone was chattering together, everyone was rushing to collect money, but no one was rushing to serve. There is no sense of boundaries and no formal five-star hotel training. At best, it is at the guest house level. The excellent quality of a very few employees cannot replace the average level. Refreshed our understanding of Shangri-La Hotel Group's services.

Meals: The coffee in the lobby bar is good, and the desserts are endless. There is a big gap between the buffet restaurant standards and prices, but the ingredients themselves are still passable and the oil used is also very good. Especially the chef in the Panini area is very clean and responsible, and the taste is very good.

The hotel has a design, but it‚Äôs so beautiful and beautiful. I‚Äôm sorry, I‚Äôve seen better ones and even more beautiful ones. But I have never stayed in a worse Shangri-La than this one.

There is a long road ahead, but I hope to move forward with dignity. Small comments cannot change a huge enterprise. The mountains are high and the road is long, no need to say goodbye.

It was rebuilt on the basis of the former factory building of Shougang, taking into account tradition and comfort, and it has a unique feeling. The room facilities are well equipped. The bathing room and the toilet room are separated without interfering with each other. There are many power outlets, which is very convenient. The breakfast category is relatively complete, and the German restaurant outside the store has a great environment. The service process is slightly inexperienced, but the staff are very enthusiastic to make up for the small shortcomings. In terms of environment, the hotel is located in the center of the Shougang Winter Olympic Park, next to the famous ski jumping platform "High Heels", and only three to four hundred meters away from the shopping center Liugonghui. The Shougang Park has undergone modernization, taking into account the orderly combination of ancient buildings, heavy industrial relics and modern lifestyles. The design sense is strong and harmonious with each other. There are tourist facilities and various restaurants. Ken McPhi is there and there are many coffee shops In Beijing's sunny winter day, although the air is a bit cooler, it is comfortable, convenient and leisurely. In addition, there are relatively few tourists, so the environment feels great.
